< text>
I loooove this hidden gem! I can‚Äôt believe I‚Äôve never heard of or been to this restaurant till now. I think it‚Äôs run by a couple and I love the personal touches. The chef is amazing - he takes your order, pours and explains the wine, and comes out to explain each course. You can choose between 3 or 5 course and a wine pairing with your meal. We did the 5 course with the wine pairing. The food was delicious and each course was nicely spaced. The wine was sooo good, and the pours were incredibly generous. We also added the corn bread pudding which was on the 3 course menu as an a la cart and that was one of my favorite dishes. The foie gras was also perfectly balanced and excellent. Definitely come here for a special, personal experience.<//text>

Carl Payne</user_name>
<Review>I went to The Richmond for a special occasion dinner and we were not let down. Nestled in the Inner Richmond next to a laundry mat isn't where one would expect to find fine dining, but The Richmond delivers. It's a small staff with the owner also working as waiter, chef, sommelier and just about anything else you could need. We had the three course tasting menu. I started with crab cakes and spinach salad which were excellent and paired with a light, crisp white. Next came duck leg with veggies and mashed potatoes paired with a GSM. Both were exceptionally prepared, presented and paired. For dessert I had the apple cobbler. Light, crisp and paired with a port, it was the perfect compliment to the meal. I highly recommend The Richmond to anyone who hasn't tried it. Somewhat pricey but very reasonable for the food and service you get. Meals are quick so expect to spent a few hours on a multi course meal.<//Review>< date>
1421522093641<//date>

<username>Eddie Torres<//username>< time>
1582563011299<//time>
<rate>4<//rate>< text>
Essentially a mini Target with a little bit of everything a full sized target would have. It's definitely smaller than the average Target; Upside: it's easy to navigate, Downside: limited product. However, they have all the basics covered from the fresh market, to CVS pharmacy, and of course, a Starbucks. Check out can get hectic during peak times due to less checkout stands but the same can be said of a regular Target: more product, more people, more check out stands, peak times will always be busy. I recommend checking the Target App to see if your product is available at this location before venturing out.< /text>

Thanks for reading and be careful dealers!

{'time': 1557873613019, 'text': "We apologize but we don't compromise on our pricing. It's called an upfront, flat-rate price. The diagnostic fee of $65 is not to 'lock you in with us' but rather to help us partially cover some of our costs of labor, our truck costs to drive out to your home, our training to diagnose the problem, etc. You are never locked in with us. We are more than willing to diagnose the problem, tell you the cost of the repair up-front, and if you don't like the pricing of the repair, you're welcome to take our knowledge of what repair is needed and do business with someone else or repair it yourself! We don't do our pricing with an hourly rate, but rather as a flate-rate price for the repair, which is an advantage to you! You know the price ahead of time, no matter how long it takes us! You don't have to hold your breath, wondering if we are dragging the job out simply to charge more, and not every knowing the cost until AFTER we are done and you're STUCK with paying it. <text>I'm going to give this particular Romano's Mac Grill a 5 star bordering on 4 tbh. 5 only bc the wait staff was very nice and extremely hard working. This particular night was semi busy. The staff worked off of each other making sure the customers were well taken care of even if they were passing by another staff's table. Very friendly and warming from all of them. And considering it was outdoors, the staff did thier best to keep our cups full.

I found it unusual that they didn't have menus and we had to look at our phones to look at thier website to see the menu. I don't particularly care for this system.

I was offered another bowl but felt I already had to much sodium for the night. <Time>1529815295223< /Time>< rating>
3<//rating>
< Review>
The service was good. No complaints there. Our waitress was friendly and attentive, and the atmosphere was nice and not too loud. For this, I give three stars instead of one.

On the other hand, the food was not so good. The bread had a good flavor but it was overwhelmingly salty. I ordered the butternut tortellacci. Honestly, with a small fraction of the salt this would probably be pretty good. It has prosciutto in it, which is already salty, so it really wasn't necessary to load it up. It totally smothered the flavor of everything else and left me with that heavy, bloated, sodium overload feeling like I just ate at Macdonald's.

My husband ordered the chicken fettuccine alfredo. It's hard to mess that up. The pasta was alright, but the chicken was both sparse and extremely poor in quality. He regretted eating it and didn't feel well afterward. So about $4 to add that gross chicken to a $13 plate of plain pasta. Not a huge plate.

So the environment was nice, and the staff, but the food was not worth it even at a cheaper price. We decided not to return before we were even out the door. Now I understand why the place was not too busy on a Saturday evening. Our loss.</Review>

< review>
I drive UberEats regularly and pickup from this Macaroni Grill pretty often. It always has alot of customers inside, but my wait for the takeout has always been just a couple of minutes until last nite. Took about 20 minutes as they were slammed. There was another UberEats driver in addition to the other delivery service drivers there, HubGrub & ? and there were also 4 customers that called in their orders for carry out.  The staff moved things along as quickly as they could to get each of us taken care of and on our way throwing in an extra something here and there or reducing the prices slightly to make up for the wait. It wasn't necessary as anyone that has ever eaten here should be aware that a busy restaurant means some amount of wait time due to the quality of food. The woman handling the orders (Yvonne) kept her composure as did the Manager (Can't remember his name). He gave me 2 different plates, a Chicken Alfredo and Lasagne for my wait. As I  said. they do see me as I said, quite often and maybe this was the reason. Both were very tasty and it was a nice gesture on his part. Now having tasted their food, I understand why the place always has alot of customers every time I'm sent there to pick up an order and I'll be taking my wife out to dinner here having sampled a very small portion of their menu. Tasty & Much appreciated.<//review>

< review>
The Macaroni Grill on Grand Oaks, Corona Ca has the WORST customer service ever. Unfortunately for us, we gave them a second chance and went there tonight. Big mistake.

My family and I (2 adults, 2 kids) were seated in the bar area, not our choice. We arrived at 7PM and waited 25 minutes, not too bad. The restaurant was extremely busy for a Friday night, first week in November.

We waited several minutes for someone to take our drink/appetizer order. Appetizers came out quick, but no silverware to eat with. By the time we got silverware, the appetizers were cold.

Eventually the bartender (cause he was the only one handling the entire bar and tables within) came to take our order, and immediately realized we never got our drinks. He took our order and returned with our drinks.

Once the food was delivered, our table was never visited again except to drop off the bill. No drink refills, no parmesan cheese to top our entre's, nothing. My wife had to visit the hostess counter on two different occasions to inquire about drink refills and bread.

There appeared to be two managers on staff tonight. We tried to get their attention as they passed by our table, (walking together deep in a conversation) it was as if what they were talking about was much more important than a paying customer who's bill was north of $80 for 4 people.

Ideally we would like our money back, but it's our fault for not leaving during the drink/appetizer debacle.

The irony is, out of all the other restaurants we frequent in (or near) the Corona Crossings Shopping center, (Kings Fish House, Wood Ranch, Miguels, Chilis, BJ's Pizza...etc), they all seem to handle a busy crowd, but for some odd reason, Macaroni Grill fails every time.

We wont be back. (Unless they read this and comp our meal, we did save our receipt)< /review>
